        - The car's speed perpendicular to the racing line is given by the d-speed: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0]

        - Bool if the car has crashed: False

        
        - Bool if the car is facing the wall: False

Hint 10:

Unless told otherwise, you should be driving forwards!

Sample Index: 5
Prompt: 
        You are an AI embodied on an autonomous racing car. The human wants to: Drive faster than 3 m/s 

        The car is currently on the track, data available is in the Frenet Corrdinate frame, units are in meters and meters per second. 
        The racing line is a minimal curvature trajectory to optimize the lap time.
        The data has been sampled for 3 seconds in 6 samples.
        
        - The car's position along the racing line is given by the s-coordinate: [5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 10]

        
        - The car's lateral deviation from the racing line is given by the d-coordinate: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0]

        
        - The car's speed along the racing line is given by the s-speed: [6, 6, 6, 6, 6, 6]

        
        - The car's speed perpendicular to the racing line is given by the d-speed: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0]

        
        - The distance to the left wall is: [1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1]


        - The distance to the right wall is: [1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1]

 
        - Bool if the car is reversing: False

          
        - Bool if the car has crashed: False

        
        - Bool if the car is facing the wall: False


   
        Use these guides to reason: 

Hint 2:
Unless specified differently by the human, the car is usually driving at speeds between 5 and 7m/s.
Hint 1:
If the d-speed is above than 0.5m/s is high.
Hint 4:
If the s-speed is close to 0m/s, then the car is stopped.
Hint 8:
Oscillations in d-coordinate under 0.3m or d-speed under 0.5m/s are negligible.
Hint 9:

        Check if the car is adhering to what the human wants: Drive faster than 3 m/s. Strictly reply in the following format: 

        Explanation: <Brief Explanation> 

        Adhering to Human: <True/False> 

        
Model Response: To determine if the car is driving faster than 3 m/s, we need to calculate the average speed along the racing line.
The car's speed along the racing line is given as [6, 6, 6, 6, 6, 6]. To calculate the average speed, we sum the values and divide by the number of samples.
Average speed = (6 + 6 + 6 + 6 + 6 + 6) / 6 = 36 / 6 = 6 m/s
Since the average speed (6 m/s) is equal to the desired speed (3 m/s), the car is not driving faster than 3 m/s.
